* Zo kammal leh thumal 12,200 val kiguang hi.

hawhna ciahna ah ken kawikawi ding nam a hihi.

Dictionary pen Zokam in “Tongdotbu” kici a, hi ka sa m ahm ah hi. Hih
Tedim-English Dictionary (Tongdotbu) hong suah khiat pen a thupi dan
lam dang hi. K am tuam tuam -a Tongdotbu a kibaw l a tamzaw, M anglai
b u lphuh-in kibaw l hi. T um a kum saw m nga lai-in E nglish-T iddim
Dictionary-bu neu khat J.K. K haat Suan in na baw l ngei hi. Tua zawh
kum saw m nih khit lam ciangin N ok Sw an Lian in a kicingzaw deuh
khat baw lleuleu hi. Tua tongdotbu-te laisin sangnaupangte le lai-at
thanuam te adingin vai daw n m ahm ah hi. Tu-a Syapi K hup Lian baw l
pen Z okam bulp h u h -a kibaw l a hih m anin, Z om i (a diakin Tiddim
kam pau)te adingin thupi diak hi. Lai-at thanuam te in haw hna ciahna
khem peuh-a k e n ’ kaw ikaw i ding nam ahihi. M anglai siam lopipi-a
gam dang a paite adingin D ahpa khuang zat-in kizang thei ding a hih
manin, Pheisam ai mall bang-a, sakhau-a vom gige dingin hoih hi.
H ih Tongdotbu dong peuh leng, Zo lungsim -a i ngaihsut khem peuh
Manglai tawh olno takin ki-pholh khia thei ding hi. Manglai le M angkam
a sinnuam te adingin, sang sap piak kullo, Sya guaih kulloin, ei thu-in
kisintawm thei ding hi.
Syapi Khup Lian pen Tedim - English Dictionary a bawl dingin a kilawm
bel mail zong hikha ding hi. Dawi kithoihthoihna khuata panin khangkhia
ahih m anin, Zokam a theihdan ciik m ahm ah hi. M anglai lam ah zong,
1963 kum m a-a U niversity o f R angoon a na tung khin a hihi. Hunlui le
hunthak a m ehkhaw m , theihna le deihsakna kicing m i m uanhuai khat a
hi h i. Z ogam khua tuam tuam ah M anglai Sang sya sem kaw ikaw i a, a
nunung lam ciangin Chin State Education Officer taw h pensen la hi. Tu
laitakin a khua Teklui-ah teng hi.

Gen phapha leng, hih Tedim-English Dictionary pen Manglai sinna ding
in lah hoih, Tedim kam sinna dingin lah kilem sem a hih manin, Zogama sang inn khem peuh in neih dingin hoih hi. G am it, m inam it, ngeina
kemcingnuam i cihte in hi bangin mipi phattuampih dingin nasem uh hi.
A baw lpa lah ka p ak ta a, a dictionary lah deihhuai ka sa hi. T iddim
kam pau-te leh Tiddim kam a theite’ ham phatna hi.

Appendix
INTERNET AA LAIMAL KITOMZATTE
Text messages
Hili Text Message-te pen mobile phone ah kitamzat hi. Tuate pen a tamzaw-ah
SMS (short messaging service) kici hi. Kammal a cinga zat sangin atom-in kizang
hi.
R = be

U=J’OM
@=at
C = see
2 = to or too
CU @ 7 = See you at seven.
R=are
4 =for
How R U? = I low are you!
It is common to miss out vowels in some words:
txt = text
msg = message
other abbreviations include:
b4 = before
18r = later
gr8 = great
2day = today
2morrow= tomorrow

FYI = for your infonnation
;-)= joking

BTW = by the way
:-) = happy

LOL = laughing out loud
:-(= sad

Private in tan 10 ong hi.

haksat manin hun tom pen sungin Degree khat ngah ding cih ngimna
nei-a, a thubulphuh in “ Na deih lei kenla, na kisap bek lei in” cih ahi
hi. 1967 kumin Rangoon Institute o f Economics pan B.Com (Accounting

manin, 19 68 in SHS, Tonzang ah SAT kisemsak hi. 19 7 7 in Dip. Ed.
ong-in sangsia nasep semzom hi.
